  )\n    ''')\n    # test_inputs table\n    c.execute('''\n        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS test_inputs (\n            id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n            client_id INTEGER,\n (\n            input_id,\n            output_file,\n            datetime.now().isoformat(),\n            json.dumps(error_categories),\n            json.dumps(errors)\n        )\n    )\n    WHERE test_inputs.client_id=?\n        ORDER BY test_outputs.analyzed_at DESC\n        LIMIT 10\n    ''', (client_id,))\n    rows = c.fetchall()\n    conn.close()\n    errors = []\n    for row in \"You are a helpful assistant for test automation.\"},\n                {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": prompt}\n            ],\n            temperature=temperature,\n            max_tokens=max_tokens\n        )\n        return response.choices[0].message['content'].strip()\n    except Exception as e:\n        print(f\"OpenAI API error: {e}\")\n        return \"\"\n\n# ==========================\n# Excel File Generation\n# ==========================\n\ndef generate_test_input_excel(client_id: int, scenario_description: str, save_path: str) -> str:\n    \"\"\"Generate Excel test input file using GPT-4.\"\"\"\n    # Build RAG context\n    recent_errors = get_recent_errors(client_id)\n    rag_context = \"\"\n    if recent_errors:\n        rag_context = \"Recent errors and categories for this client:\\n\"\n        for err in recent_errors:\n            rag_context += f\"- Categories: {', '.join(err['categories'])}\\n\"\n            rag_context += f\"  Errors: {', '.join(err['errors'])}\\n\"\n    prompt = (\n        f\"{rag_context}\\n\"\n        f\"Given the following test scenario description, generate a table in CSV format. \"\n        f\"Each row is a test case. Include columns for 'TestCaseID', 'Input1', 'Input2', 'ExpectedOutput'.\\n\"\n        f\"Scenario: {scenario_description}\\n\"\n        f\"Generate at least 5 test cases.\"\n    )\n    csv_content = gpt4_generate(prompt)\n    if not csv_content:\n        raise RuntimeError(\"Failed to generate test input via GPT-4.\")\n    # Save CSV to Excel\n    with tempfile.NamedTemporaryFile(delete=False, suffix=\".csv\", mode=\"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as tmp_csv:\n        tmp_csv.write(csv_content)\n        tmp_csv_path = tmp_csv.name\n    try:\n        df = pd.read_csv(tmp_csv_path)\n        df.to_excel(save_path, index=False)\n    finally:\n        os.unlink(tmp_csv_path)\n    # Save prompt for traceability\n    return prompt\n\n# ==========================\n# Output Analysis\n# GPT-4.\"\"\"\n    df_input = pd.read_excel(input_excel)\n    df_output = pd.read_excel(output_excel)\n    # Merge on TestCaseID\n    merged = pd.merge(df_input, df_output, on=\"TestCaseID\", suffixes=('_in', '_out'), how='left')\n    errors = []\n    for idx, row in merged.iterrows():\n        expected = row.get('ExpectedOutput_in')\n        actual = row.get('ExpectedOutput_out')\n        if pd.isna(actual) or expected != actual:\n            errors.append({\n                \"TestCaseID\": row['TestCaseID'],\n                \"Expected\": expected,\n                \"Actual\": actual\n            })\n    # Ask GPT-4 to categorize errors\n    error_descriptions = [f\"TestCaseID {e['TestCaseID']}: expected {e['Expected']}, got {e['Actual']}\" for e in errors]\n    if errors:\n        prompt = (\n            \"Given these test case errors, categorize the errors and summarize the main error types. \"\n            \"List categories as a Python list of strings.\\n\"\n            \"Errors:\\n\" +\n            \"\\n\".join(error_descriptions)\n        )\n        categories = gpt4_generate(prompt)\n        try:\n            # Try to parse as Python list\n            categories_list = eval(categories)\n            if not isinstance(categories_list, list):\n                categories_list = [categories]\n        except Exception:\n            categories_list = [categories]\n    else:\n        categories_list = []\n    return {\n        \"error_categories\": categories_list,\n        \"errors\": error_descriptions\n    }\n\n# ==========================\n#                         "import os\nimport sys\nimport json\nimport time\nimport sqlite3\nimport openai\nimport traceback\nimport threading\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional\nfrom datetime str:\n    \"\"\"Send prompt to GPT-4 and return the response.\"\"\"\n    openai.api_key = OPENAI_API_KEY\n    try:\n        response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(\n            model=\"gpt-4\",\n            messages=[{\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": prompt}],\n            max_tokens=max_tokens,\n            temperature=0.2,\n        )\n        return cases using GPT-4, optionally using previous error data to improve the cases.\n    \"\"\"\n    prompt = (\n        f\"You are to generate input data for automated test scenarios for client \"Previous errors encountered include:\\n\" +\n            \"\\n\".join([f\"- {e['error_message']}\" for e in previous_errors]) +\n            \"\\nPlease generate new test cases that avoid these           FOREIGN KEY(client_id) REFERENCES clients(id)\n            )\n        ''')\n        # Table for errors\n        c.execute('''\n            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS errors (\n                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n                scenario_id INTEGER,\n                error_type TEXT,\n                error_details TEXT,\n                occurred_at TEXT,\n                FOREIGN KEY(scenario_id) REFERENCES test_scenarios(id)\n            )\n        ''')\n        self.conn.commit()\n\n    def get_or_create_client(self, name: str) -> int:\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute(\"SELECT id FROM clients WHERE name = ?\", (name,))\n        row = c.fetchone()\n        if row:\n            return row[0]\n        c.execute(\"INSERT INTO clients (name) VALUES (?)\", (name,))\n        self.conn.commit()\n        return c.lastrowid\n\n    def log_scenario(self, client_id: int, input_file: str, output_file: str, prompt: str, response: str) -> int:\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute('''\n            INSERT INTO test_scenarios (client_id, input_file, output_file, gpt_prompt, gpt_response, generated_at)\n            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\n        ''', (client_id, input_file, output_file, prompt, response, datetime.now().isoformat()))\n        self.conn.commit()\n        return c.lastrowid\n\n    def log_error(self, scenario_id: int, error_type: str, error_details: str):\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute('''\n            INSERT INTO errors (scenario_id, error_type, error_details, occurred_at)\n            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)\n        ''', (scenario_id, error_type, error_details, datetime.now().isoformat()))\n        self.conn.commit()\n\n    def get_recent_errors(self, client_id: int, limit: int = 10) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute('''\n            SELECT e.error_type, e.error_details, e.occurred_at\n            FROM errors e\n            JOIN test_scenarios s ON e.scenario_id = s.id\n            WHERE s.client_id = ?\n            ORDER BY e.occurred_at DESC\n            LIMIT ?\n        ''', (client_id, limit))\n        return [{\"type\": row[0], \"details\": row[1], \"when\": row[2]} for row in c.fetchall()]\n\n    def close(self):\n        self.conn.close()\n\n# -------------------- GPT-4 API LAYER --------------------\n\nclass GPT4Generator:\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str):\n        openai.api_key = api_key\n\n    def generate_input_excel(self, prompt: str) -> pd.DataFrame:\n        \"\"\"\n        Use GPT-4 to generate tabular test input data.\n        Returns a pandas DataFrame.\n        \"\"\"\n        logging.info(\"Sending prompt to GPT-4: %s\", prompt)\n        try:\n            response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(\n                model=\"gpt-4\",\n                messages=[\n                    {\"role\": \"system\", \"content\": \"You are a helpful assistant that generates test scenario data in CSV format.\"},\n                    {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": prompt}\n                ],\n                max_tokens=1200,\n                temperature=0.2\n            )\n            csv_text = response['choices'][0]['message']['content']\n            df = pd.read_csv(pd.compat.StringIO(csv_text))\n            return df, csv_text\n        except Exception as e:\n            logging.error(\"GPT-4 generation failed: %s\", str(e))\n            raise\n\n# -------------------- ANALYSIS & ERROR CATEGORIZATION --------------------\n\ndef analyze_output(input_df: pd.DataFrame, output_df: pd.DataFrame) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Analyze the output file, compare with input, and categorize errors.\n    Returns a list of error dicts.\n    \"\"\"\n    errors = []\n    # Example: Check for missing columns\n    for col in input_df.columns:\n        if col not in output_df.columns:\n            errors.append({\n                \"type\": \"MissingColumn\",\n                \"details\": f\"Column '{col}' is missing in output.\"\n            })\n    # Example: Check for row count mismatch\n    if len(input_df) != len(output_df):\n        errors.append({\n            \"type\": \"RowCountMismatch\",\n            \"details\": f\"Input rows: {len(input_df)}, Output rows: {len(output_df)}\"\n        })\n    # Example: Check for value mismatches\n    common_cols = [col for col in input_df.columns if col in output_df.columns]\n    for col in common_cols:\n        for idx, (in_val, out_val) in enumerate(zip(input_df[col], output_df[col])):\n            if in_val != out_val:\n                errors.append({\n                    \"type\": \"ValueMismatch\",\n                    \"details\": f\"Row {idx}, Column '{col}': input='{in_val}' output='{out_val}'\"\n                })\n    return errors\n\n# -------------------- IMPROVEMENT LOGIC --------------------\n\ndef build_gpt_prompt(client_name: str, previous_errors: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> str:\n    \"\"\"\n    Build a prompt for GPT-4, taking into account previous errors for improvement.\n    \"\"\"\n    prompt = f\"Generate a new Excel test input file for automated test scenarios for client '{client_name}'.\"\n    if previous_errors:\n        prompt += \"\\nPrevious errors to avoid:\\n\"\n        for err in previous_errors:\n            prompt += f\"- {err['type']}: {err['details']}\\n\"\n    prompt += \"\\nThe file should have at least 5 rows and 3-5 columns, with realistic test data.\"\n    prompt += \"\\nOutput the data as CSV (with header row).\"\n    return prompt\n\n# -------------------- FILE UTILITIES --------------------\n\ndef save_dataframe_to_excel(df: pd.DataFrame, file_path:     except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"GPT-4 Error\", f\"Failed to generate input: {e}\")\n            return\n        # Save file\n        file_name = \"\"\"Handles SQLite-based RAG knowledge base for multi-client scenarios.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, db_file=DB_FILE):\n        self.conn = sqlite3.connect(db_file, check_same_thread=False)\n        self._init_db()\n\n    def _init_db(self):\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute('''\n            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS clients (\n                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n                name TEXT UNIQUE\n            )\n        ''')\n        c.execute('''\n            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS test_scenarios (\n                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n                client_id INTEGER,\n                input_file TEXT,\n                output_file TEXT,\n                gpt_prompt TEXT,\n                gpt_response TEXT,\n                generated_at TEXT,\n                FOREIGN KEY(client_id) REFERENCES clients(id)\n            )\n        ''')\n        c.execute('''\n            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS errors (\n                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n                scenario_id INTEGER,\n                error_type TEXT,\n                error_details TEXT,\n                occurred_at TEXT,\n                FOREIGN KEY(scenario_id) REFERENCES test_scenarios(id)\n            )\n        ''')\n        self.conn.commit()\n\n    def get_or_create_client(self, name: str) -> int:\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute(\"SELECT id FROM clients WHERE name = ?\", (name,))\n        row = c.fetchone()\n        if row:\n            return row[0]\n        c.execute(\"INSERT INTO clients (name) VALUES (?)\", (name,))\n        self.conn.commit()\n        return c.lastrowid\n\n    def log_scenario(self, client_id: int, input_file: str, output_file: Optional[str], prompt: str, response: str) -> int:\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute('''\n            INSERT INTO test_scenarios (client_id, input_file, output_file, gpt_prompt, gpt_response, generated_at)\n            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\n        ''', (client_id, input_file, output_file, prompt, response, datetime.now().isoformat()))\n        self.conn.commit()\n        return c.lastrowid\n\n    def log_error(self, scenario_id: int, error_type: str, error_details: str):\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute('''\n            INSERT INTO errors (scenario_id, error_type, error_details, occurred_at)\n            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)\n        ''', (scenario_id, error_type, error_details, datetime.now().isoformat()))\n        self.conn.commit()\n\n    def get_recent_errors(self, client_id: int, limit: int = 10) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute('''\n            SELECT e.error_type, e.error_details, e.occurred_at\n            FROM errors e\n            JOIN test_scenarios s ON e.scenario_id = s.id\n            WHERE s.client_id = ?\n            ORDER BY e.occurred_at DESC\n            LIMIT ?\n        ''', (client_id, limit))\n        return [{\"type\": row[0], \"details\": row[1], \"when\": row[2]} for row in c.fetchall()]\n\n    def update_output_file(self, scenario_id: int, output_file: str):\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute(\"UPDATE test_scenarios SET output_file = ? WHERE id = ?\", (output_file, scenario_id))\n        self.conn.commit()\n\n    def find_scenario_by_input(self, input_file: str) -> Optional[int]:\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute(\"SELECT id FROM test_scenarios WHERE input_file = ?\", (input_file,))\n        row = c.fetchone()\n        return row[0] if row else None\n\n    def close(self):\n        self.conn.close()\n\n# -------------------- GPT-4 API LAYER --------------------\n\nclass GPT4Generator:\n    \"\"\"Handles GPT-4 API calls for generating test scenario input data.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str):\n        openai.api_key = api_key\n\n    def generate_input_excel(self, prompt: str) -> (pd.DataFrame, str):\n        \"\"\"\n        Use GPT-4 to generate tabular test input data.\n        Returns a pandas DataFrame and the raw CSV text.\n        \"\"\"\n        logging.info(\"Sending prompt to GPT-4: %s\", prompt)\n        try:\n            response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(\n                model=\"gpt-4\",\n                messages=[\n                    {\"role\": \"system\", \"content\": \"You are a helpful assistant that generates test scenario data in CSV format.\"},\n                    {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": prompt}\n                ],\n                max_tokens=1200,\n                temperature=0.2\n            )\n            csv_text = response['choices'][0]['message']['content']\n            # Use StringIO to read CSV from string\n            from io import StringIO\n            df = pd.read_csv(StringIO(csv_text))\n            return df, csv_text\n        except Exception as e:\n            logging.error(\"GPT-4 generation failed: %s\", str(e))\n            raise\n\n# -------------------- ANALYSIS & ERROR CATEGORIZATION --------------------\n\ndef analyze_output(input_df: pd.DataFrame, output_df: pd.DataFrame) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Analyze the output file, compare with input, and categorize errors.\n    Returns a list of error dicts.\n    \"\"\"\n    errors = []\n    # Check for missing columns\n    for col in input_df.columns:\n        if col not in output_df.columns:\n            errors.append({\n                \"type\": \"MissingColumn\",\n                \"details\": f\"Column '{col}' is missing in output.\"\n            })\n    # Check for row count mismatch\n    if len(input_df) != len(output_df):\n        errors.append({\n            \"type\": \"RowCountMismatch\",\n            \"details\": f\"Input rows: {len(input_df)}, Output rows: {len(output_df)}\"\n        })\n    # Check for value mismatches\n    common_cols = [col for col in input_df.columns if col in output_df.columns]\n    for col in common_cols:\n        for idx, (in_val, out_val) in enumerate(zip(input_df[col], output_df[col])):\n            if pd.isnull(in_val) and pd.isnull(out_val):\n                continue\n            if in_val != out_val:\n                errors.append({\n                    \"type\": \"ValueMismatch\",\n                    \"details\": f\"Row {idx+1}, Column '{col}': input='{in_val}' output='{out_val}'\"\n                })\n    return errors\n\n# -------------------- IMPROVEMENT LOGIC --------------------\n\ndef build_gpt_prompt(client_name: str, previous_errors: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> str:\n    \"\"\"\n    Build a prompt for GPT-4, taking into account previous errors for improvement.\n    \"\"\"\n    prompt = f\"Generate a new Excel test input file for automated test scenarios for client '{client_name}'.\"\n    if previous_errors:\n        prompt += \"\\nPrevious errors to avoid:\\n\"\n        for err in previous_errors:\n            prompt += f\"- {err['type']}: {err['details']}\\n\"\n    prompt += \"\\nThe file should have at least 5 rows and 3-5 columns, with realistic test data.\"\n    prompt += \"\\nOutput the data as CSV (with header row).\"\n    return prompt\n\n# -------------------- FILE UTILITIES --------------------\n\ndef save_dataframe_to_excel(df: pd.DataFrame, file_path: Path):\n    \"\"\"Save DataFrame to Excel file.\"\"\"\n    df.to_excel(file_path, index=False)\n\ndef load_excel_to_dataframe(file_path: Path) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"Load Excel file into DataFrame.\"\"\"\n    return pd.read_excel(file_path)\n\n# -------------------- MULTI-CLIENT SUPPORT & UI --------------------\n\nclass TestScenarioApp:\n    \"\"\"Main application class with Tkinter UI.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, master):\n        self.master = master\n        self.master.title(\"GPT-4 Test Scenario Generator\")\n        self.kb = RAGKnowledgeBase()\n        self.gpt = GPT4Generator(OPENAI_API_KEY)\n\n        self.selected_client: Optional[str] = None\n        self.client_id: Optional[int] = None\n\n        self._build_ui()\n\n    def _build_ui(self):\n        # Client selection\n        tk.Label(self.master, text=\"Client Name:\").grid(row=0, column=0, sticky=\"e\")\n        self.client_entry = tk.Entry(self.master)\n        self.client_entry.grid(row=0, column=1, sticky=\"w\")\n        tk.Button(self.master, text=\"Set Client\", command=self.set_client).grid(row=0, column=2)\n\n        # Generate input\n        self.gen_btn = tk.Button(self.master, text=\"Generate Input Excel\", command=self.generate_input, state=tk.DISABLED)\n        self.gen_btn.grid(row=1, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=5, sticky=\"ew\")\n\n        # Analyze output\n        tk.Button(self.master, text=\"Analyze Output Excel\", command=self.analyze_output).grid(row=2, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=5, sticky=\"ew\")\n\n        # Recent errors\n        tk.Button(self.master, text=\"Show Recent Errors\", command=self.show_recent_errors).grid(row=3, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=5, sticky=\"ew\")\n\n        # Exit\n        tk.Button(self.master, text=\"Quit\", command=self.quit).grid(row=4, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=5, sticky=\"ew\")\n\n    def set_client(self):\n        name = self.client_entry.get().strip()\n        if not name:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Please enter a client name.\")\n            return\n        self.selected_client = name\n        self.client_id = self.kb.get_or_create_client(name)\n        self.gen_btn.config(state=tk.NORMAL)\n        messagebox.showinfo(\"Client Set\", f\"Client '{name}' selected.\")\n\n    def generate_input(self):\n        if not self.selected_client or self.client_id is None:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Set a client first.\")\n            return\n        prev_errors = self.kb.get_recent_errors(self.client_id)\n        prompt = build_gpt_prompt(self.selected_client, prev_errors)\n        try:\n            df, gpt_response = self.gpt.generate_input_excel(prompt)\n        except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"GPT-4 Error\", f\"Failed to generate input: {e}\")\n            return\n        # Save file\n        file_name = f\"{self.selected_client}_input_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.xlsx\"\n        file_path = DATA_DIR / file_name\n        try:\n            save_dataframe_to_excel(df, file_path)\n        except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"File Error\", f\"Failed to save Excel file: {e}\")\n            return\n        # Log scenario\n        scenario_id = self.kb.log_scenario(self.client_id, str(file_path), None, prompt, gpt_response)\n        messagebox.showinfo(\"Input Generated\", f\"Input Excel file saved as:\\n{file_path}\")\n\n    def analyze_output(self):\n        if not self.selected_client or self.client_id is None:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Set a client first.\")\n            return\n        # Select input and output files\n        input_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(title=\"Select Input Excel\", filetypes=[(\"Excel files\", \"*.xlsx\")])\n        if not input_path:\n            return\n        output_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(title=\"Select Output Excel\", filetypes=[(\"Excel files\", \"*.xlsx\")])\n        if not output_path:\n            return\n        try:\n            input_df = load_excel_to_dataframe(input_path)\n            output_df = load_excel_to_dataframe(output_path)\n        except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", f\"Failed to load files: {e}\")\n            return\n        errors = analyze_output(input_df, output_df)\n        # Find scenario\n        scenario_id = self.kb.find_scenario_by_input(input_path)\n        # Log errors\n        for err in errors:\n            if scenario_id:\n                self.kb.log_error(scenario_id, err['type'], err['details'])\n        # Update output file path in scenario\n        if scenario_id:\n            self.kb.update_output_file(scenario_id, output_path)\n        if errors:\n            msg = f\"Errors found:\\n\" + \"\\n\".join([f\"{e['type']}: {e['details']}\" for e in errors])\n            messagebox.showwarning(\"Analysis Result\", msg)\n        else:\n            messagebox.showinfo(\"Analysis Result\", \"No errors found.\")\n\n    def show_recent_errors(self):\n        if not self.selected_client or self.client_id is None:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Set a client first.\")\n            return\n        errors = self.kb.get_recent_errors(self.client_id, limit=10)\n        if not errors:\n            messagebox.showinfo(\"Recent Errors\", \"No errors found for this client.\")\n            return\n        msg = \"\\n\".join([f\"{e['when']}: {e['type']} - {e['details']}\" for e in errors])\n        messagebox.showinfo(\"Recent Errors\", msg)\n\n    def quit(self):\n        self.kb.close()\n        self.master.quit()\n\n# -------------------- ENTRY POINT --------------------\n\ndef main():\n    DATA_DIR.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n    root = tk.Tk()\n    app = self.conn.commit()\n        return c.lastrowid\n\n    def log_error(self, scenario_id: int, error_type: str, error_details: str):\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute('''\n analyze_output(input_df: pd.DataFrame, output_df: pd.DataFrame):\n    errors = []\n    # Check for missing columns\n    for col in input_df.columns:\n        if col not in output_df.columns:\n            errors.append({\n                \"type\": \"MissingColumn\",\n                \"details\": f\"Column '{col}' is missing in output.\"\n            })\n    # Check for row count mismatch\n    if len(input_df) != len(output_df):\n        errors.append({\n            \"type\": \"RowCountMismatch\",\n            \"details\": f\"Input rows: {len(input_df)}, Output rows: {len(output_df)}\"\n        })\n    # Check for value mismatches\n    common_cols = [col for col in input_df.columns if col in output_df.columns]\n    for col in common_cols:\n        for idx, (in_val, out_val) in     ''')\n        c.execute('''\n            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS test_scenarios (\n                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n                client_id INTEGER,\n            )\n        ''')\n        self.conn.commit()\n\n    def get_or_create_client(self, name: str) -> int:\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute(\"SELECT id FROM clients WHERE name = output file, compare with input, and categorize errors.\n    Returns a list of error dicts.\n    \"\"\"\n    errors = []\n    # Check for missing columns\n    for col in input_df.columns:\n        if prev_errors)\n        try:\n            df, gpt_response = self.gpt.generate_input_excel(prompt)\n        except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"GPT-4 Error\", f\"Failed to generate input: {e}\")\n            return\n        # Save file\n        file_name = f\"{self.selected_client}_input_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.xlsx\"\n        file_path = DATA_DIR / file_name\n        try:\n            save_dataframe_to_excel(df, file_path)\n        except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"File Error\", f\"Failed to save Excel file: {e}\")\n            return\n        # Log scenario\n        scenario_id = self.kb.log_scenario(self.client_id, str(file_path), None, prompt, gpt_response)\n        messagebox.showinfo(\"Input Generated\", f\"Input Excel file saved as:\\n{file_path}\")\n\n    def analyze_output(self):\n        if not self.selected_client or self.client_id is None:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Set a client first.\")\n            return\n        # Select input and output files\n        input_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(title=\"Select Input Excel\", filetypes=[(\"Excel files\", \"*.xlsx\")])\n        if not input_path:\n            return\n        output_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(title=\"Select Output Excel\", filetypes=[(\"Excel files\", \"*.xlsx\")])\n        if not output_path:\n            return\n        try:\n            input_df = load_excel_to_dataframe(input_path)\n            output_df = load_excel_to_dataframe(output_path)\n        except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", f\"Failed to load files: {e}\")\n            return\n        errors = analyze_output(input_df, output_df)\n        # Find scenario\n        scenario_id = self.kb.find_scenario_by_input(input_path)\n        # Log errors\n        for err in errors:\n            if scenario_id:\n                self.kb.log_error(scenario_id, err['type'], err['details'])\n        # Update output file path in scenario\n        if scenario_id:\n            self.kb.update_output_file(scenario_id, output_path)\n        if errors:\n            msg = f\"Errors found:\\n\" + \"\\n\".join([f\"{e['type']}: {e['details']}\" for e in errors])\n            messagebox.showwarning(\"Analysis Result\", msg)\n        else:\n            messagebox.showinfo(\"Analysis Result\", \"No errors found.\")\n\n    def show_recent_errors(self):\n        if not self.selected_client or self.client_id is None:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Set a client first.\")\n            return\n        errors = self.kb.get_recent_errors(self.client_id, limit=10)\n        if not errors:\n            messagebox.showinfo(\"Recent Errors\", \"No errors found for this client.\")\n            return\n        msg = \"\\n\".join([f\"{e['when']}: {e['type']} - {e['details']}\" for e in errors])\n        messagebox.showinfo(\"Recent Errors\", msg)\n\n    def quit(self):\n        self.kb.close()\n        self.master.quit()\n\n# -------------------- ENTRY POINT --------------------\n\ndef main():\n    DATA_DIR.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n    root = tk.Tk()\n    app = TestScenarioApp(root)\n    root.mainloop()\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    main()\n\n# -------------------- PACKAGING INSTRUCTIONS --------------------\n# To create a standalone .exe, install                         "import os\nimport sys\nimport openai\nimport sqlite3\nimport logging\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom typing import List, Dict, Any, Optional\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nimport tkinter as tk\nfrom tkinter import filedialog, messagebox\n\nimport pandas as pd\n\n# -------------------- CONFIGURATION --------------------\n\n# Set your OpenAI API key here or set the environment variable OPENAI_API_KEY\nOPENAI_API_KEY = os.getenv(\"OPENAI_API_KEY\", \"sk-...\")  # <-- Replace with your key or use env variable\n\n# Database file\nDB_FILE = \"rag_knowledge_base.db\"\n\n# Directory to store generated input/output files\nDATA_DIR = Path(\"client_data\")\nDATA_DIR.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n\n# Logging setup\nlogging.basicConfig(\n    filename='app.log', \n    level=logging.INFO,\n    format='%(asctime)s %(levelname)s %(message)s'\n)\n\n# -------------------- DATABASE LAYER --------------------\n\nclass RAGKnowledgeBase:\n    \"\"\"Handles SQLite-based RAG knowledge base for multi-client scenarios.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, db_file=DB_FILE):\n        self.conn = sqlite3.connect(db_file, check_same_thread=False)\n        self._init_db()\n\n    def _init_db(self):\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute('''\n            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS clients (\n                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n                name TEXT UNIQUE\n            )\n        ''')\n        c.execute('''\n            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS test_scenarios (\n                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n                client_id INTEGER,\n                input_file TEXT,\n                output_file TEXT,\n                gpt_prompt TEXT,\n                gpt_response TEXT,\n                generated_at TEXT,\n                FOREIGN KEY(client_id) REFERENCES clients(id)\n            )\n        ''')\n        c.execute('''\n            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS errors (\n                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n                scenario_id INTEGER,\n                error_type TEXT,\n                error_details TEXT,\n                occurred_at TEXT,\n                FOREIGN KEY(scenario_id) REFERENCES test_scenarios(id)\n            )\n        ''')\n        self.conn.commit()\n\n    def get_or_create_client(self, name: str) -> int:\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute(\"SELECT id FROM clients WHERE name = ?\", (name,))\n        row = c.fetchone()\n        if row:\n            return row[0]\n        c.execute(\"INSERT INTO clients (name) VALUES (?)\", (name,))\n        self.conn.commit()\n        return c.lastrowid\n\n    def log_scenario(self, client_id: int, input_file: str, output_file: Optional[str], prompt: str, response: str) -> int:\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute('''\n            INSERT INTO test_scenarios (client_id, input_file, output_file, gpt_prompt, gpt_response, generated_at)\n            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\n        ''', (client_id, input_file, output_file, prompt, response, datetime.now().isoformat()))\n        self.conn.commit()\n        return c.lastrowid\n\n    def log_error(self, scenario_id: int, error_type: str, error_details: str):\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute('''\n            INSERT INTO errors (scenario_id, error_type, error_details, occurred_at)\n            VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?)\n        ''', (scenario_id, error_type, error_details, datetime.now().isoformat()))\n        self.conn.commit()\n\n    def get_recent_errors(self, client_id: int, limit: int = 10) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute('''\n            SELECT e.error_type, e.error_details, e.occurred_at\n            FROM errors e\n            JOIN test_scenarios s ON e.scenario_id = s.id\n            WHERE s.client_id = ?\n            ORDER BY e.occurred_at DESC\n            LIMIT ?\n        ''', (client_id, limit))\n        return [{\"type\": row[0], \"details\": row[1], \"when\": row[2]} for row in c.fetchall()]\n\n    def update_output_file(self, scenario_id: int, output_file: str):\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute(\"UPDATE test_scenarios SET output_file = ? WHERE id = ?\", (output_file, scenario_id))\n        self.conn.commit()\n\n    def find_scenario_by_input(self, input_file: str) -> Optional[int]:\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute(\"SELECT id FROM test_scenarios WHERE input_file = ?\", (input_file,))\n        row = c.fetchone()\n        return row[0] if row else None\n\n    def close(self):\n        self.conn.close()\n\n# -------------------- GPT-4 API LAYER --------------------\n\nclass GPT4Generator:\n    \"\"\"Handles GPT-4 API calls for generating test scenario input data.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, api_key: str):\n        openai.api_key = api_key\n\n    def generate_input_excel(self, prompt: str) -> (pd.DataFrame, str):\n        \"\"\"\n        Use GPT-4 to generate tabular test input data.\n        Returns a pandas DataFrame and the raw CSV text.\n        \"\"\"\n        logging.info(\"Sending prompt to GPT-4: %s\", prompt)\n        try:\n            response = openai.ChatCompletion.create(\n                model=\"gpt-4\",\n                messages=[\n                    {\"role\": \"system\", \"content\": \"You are a helpful assistant that generates test scenario data in CSV format.\"},\n                    {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": prompt}\n                ],\n                max_tokens=1200,\n                temperature=0.2\n            )\n            csv_text = response['choices'][0]['message']['content']\n            # Use StringIO to read CSV from string\n            from io import StringIO\n            df = pd.read_csv(StringIO(csv_text))\n            return df, csv_text\n        except Exception as e:\n            logging.error(\"GPT-4 generation failed: %s\", str(e))\n            raise\n\n# -------------------- ANALYSIS & ERROR CATEGORIZATION --------------------\n\ndef analyze_output(input_df: pd.DataFrame, output_df: pd.DataFrame) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:\n    \"\"\"\n    Analyze the output file, compare with input, and categorize errors.\n    Returns a list of error dicts.\n    \"\"\"\n    errors = []\n    # Check for missing columns\n    for col in input_df.columns:\n        if col not in output_df.columns:\n            errors.append({\n                \"type\": \"MissingColumn\",\n                \"details\": f\"Column '{col}' is missing in output.\"\n            })\n    # Check for row count mismatch\n    if len(input_df) != len(output_df):\n        errors.append({\n            \"type\": \"RowCountMismatch\",\n            \"details\": f\"Input rows: {len(input_df)}, Output rows: {len(output_df)}\"\n        })\n    # Check for value mismatches\n    common_cols = [col for col in input_df.columns if col in output_df.columns]\n    for col in common_cols:\n        for idx, (in_val, out_val) in enumerate(zip(input_df[col], output_df[col])):\n            if pd.isnull(in_val) and pd.isnull(out_val):\n                continue\n            if in_val != out_val:\n                errors.append({\n                    \"type\": \"ValueMismatch\",\n                    \"details\": f\"Row {idx+1}, Column '{col}': input='{in_val}' output='{out_val}'\"\n                })\n    return errors\n\n# -------------------- IMPROVEMENT LOGIC --------------------\n\ndef build_gpt_prompt(client_name: str, previous_errors: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> str:\n    \"\"\"\n    Build a prompt for GPT-4, taking into account previous errors for improvement.\n    \"\"\"\n    prompt = f\"Generate a new Excel test input file for automated test scenarios for client '{client_name}'.\"\n    if previous_errors:\n        prompt += \"\\nPrevious errors to avoid:\\n\"\n        for err in previous_errors:\n            prompt += f\"- {err['type']}: {err['details']}\\n\"\n    prompt += \"\\nThe file should have at least 5 rows and 3-5 columns, with realistic test data.\"\n    prompt += \"\\nOutput the data as CSV (with header row).\"\n    return prompt\n\n# -------------------- FILE UTILITIES --------------------\n\ndef save_dataframe_to_excel(df: pd.DataFrame, file_path: Path):\n    \"\"\"Save DataFrame to Excel file.\"\"\"\n    df.to_excel(file_path, index=False)\n\ndef load_excel_to_dataframe(file_path: Path) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"Load Excel file into DataFrame.\"\"\"\n    return pd.read_excel(file_path)\n\n# -------------------- MULTI-CLIENT SUPPORT & UI --------------------\n\nclass TestScenarioApp:\n    \"\"\"Main application class with Tkinter UI.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, master):\n        self.master = master\n        self.master.title(\"GPT-4 Test Scenario Generator\")\n        self.kb = RAGKnowledgeBase()\n        self.gpt = GPT4Generator(OPENAI_API_KEY)\n\n        self.selected_client: Optional[str] = None\n        self.client_id: Optional[int] = None\n\n        self._build_ui()\n\n    def _build_ui(self):\n        # Client selection\n        tk.Label(self.master, text=\"Client Name:\").grid(row=0, column=0, sticky=\"e\")\n        self.client_entry = tk.Entry(self.master)\n        self.client_entry.grid(row=0, column=1, sticky=\"w\")\n        tk.Button(self.master, text=\"Set Client\", command=self.set_client).grid(row=0, column=2)\n\n        # Generate input\n        self.gen_btn = tk.Button(self.master, text=\"Generate Input Excel\", command=self.generate_input, state=tk.DISABLED)\n        self.gen_btn.grid(row=1, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=5, sticky=\"ew\")\n\n        # Analyze output\n        tk.Button(self.master, text=\"Analyze Output Excel\", command=self.analyze_output).grid(row=2, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=5, sticky=\"ew\")\n\n        # Recent errors\n        tk.Button(self.master, text=\"Show Recent Errors\", command=self.show_recent_errors).grid(row=3, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=5, sticky=\"ew\")\n\n        # Exit\n        tk.Button(self.master, text=\"Quit\", command=self.quit).grid(row=4, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=5, sticky=\"ew\")\n\n    def set_client(self):\n        name = self.client_entry.get().strip()\n        if not name:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Please enter a client name.\")\n            return\n        self.selected_client = name\n        self.client_id = self.kb.get_or_create_client(name)\n        self.gen_btn.config(state=tk.NORMAL)\n        messagebox.showinfo(\"Client Set\", f\"Client '{name}' selected.\")\n\n    def generate_input(self):\n        if not self.selected_client or self.client_id is None:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Set a client first.\")\n            return\n        prev_errors = self.kb.get_recent_errors(self.client_id)\n        prompt = build_gpt_prompt(self.selected_client, prev_errors)\n        try:\n            df, gpt_response = self.gpt.generate_input_excel(prompt)\n        except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"GPT-4 Error\", f\"Failed to        return\n        # Log scenario\n        scenario_id = self.kb.log_scenario(self.client_id, str(file_path), None, prompt, gpt_response)\n        messagebox.showinfo(\"Input Generated\", f\"Input file should have at least 5 rows and 3-5 columns, with realistic test data.\"\n    prompt += \"\\nOutput the data as CSV (with header row).\"\n    return prompt\n\n# -------------------- FILE load_excel_to_dataframe(file_path: Path) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"Load Excel file into DataFrame.\"\"\"\n    return pd.read_excel(file_path)\n\n# -------------------- MULTI-CLIENT SUPPORT & UI state=tk.DISABLED)\n        self.gen_btn.grid(row=1, column=0, columnspan=3, pady=5, sticky=\"ew\")\n\n        # Analyze output\n        tk.Button(self.master, text=\"Analyze Output Excel\", client name.\")\n            return\n        self.selected_client = name\n        self.client_id = self.kb.get_or_create_client(name)\n        self.gen_btn.config(state=tk.NORMAL)\n messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Set a client first.\")\n            return\n        prev_errors = self.kb.get_recent_errors(self.client_id)\n        prompt = build_gpt_prompt(self.selected_client, prev_errors)\n        try:\n            df, gpt_response = self.gpt.generate_input_excel(prompt)\n        except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"GPT-4 Error\", f\"Failed to generate input: {e}\")\n            return\n        # Save file\n        file_name = f\"{self.selected_client}_input_{datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')}.xlsx\"\n        file_path = DATA_DIR / file_name\n        try:\n            save_dataframe_to_excel(df, file_path)\n        except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"File Error\", f\"Failed to save Excel file: {e}\")\n            return\n        # Log scenario\n        scenario_id = self.kb.log_scenario(self.client_id, str(file_path), None, prompt, gpt_response)\n        messagebox.showinfo(\"Input Generated\", f\"Input Excel file saved as:\\n{file_path}\")\n\n    def analyze_output(self):\n        if not self.selected_client or self.client_id is None:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Set a client first.\")\n            return\n        # Select input and output files\n        input_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(title=\"Select Input Excel\", filetypes=[(\"Excel files\", \"*.xlsx\")])\n        if not input_path:\n            return\n        output_path = filedialog.askopenfilename(title=\"Select Output Excel\", filetypes=[(\"Excel files\", \"*.xlsx\")])\n        if not output_path:\n            return\n        try:\n            input_df = load_excel_to_dataframe(input_path)\n            output_df = load_excel_to_dataframe(output_path)\n        except Exception as e:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", f\"Failed to load files: {e}\")\n            return\n        errors = analyze_output(input_df, output_df)\n        # Find scenario\n        scenario_id = self.kb.find_scenario_by_input(input_path)\n        # Log errors\n        for err in errors:\n            if scenario_id:\n                self.kb.log_error(scenario_id, err['type'], err['details'])\n        # Update output file path in scenario\n        if scenario_id:\n            self.kb.update_output_file(scenario_id, output_path)\n        if errors:\n            msg = f\"Errors found:\\n\" + \"\\n\".join([f\"{e['type']}: {e['details']}\" for e in errors])\n            messagebox.showwarning(\"Analysis Result\", msg)\n        else:\n            messagebox.showinfo(\"Analysis Result\", \"No errors found.\")\n\n    def show_recent_errors(self):\n        if not self.selected_client or self.client_id is None:\n            messagebox.showerror(\"Error\", \"Set a client first.\")\n            return\n        errors = self.kb.get_recent_errors(self.client_id, limit=10)\n        if not errors:\n            messagebox.showinfo(\"Recent Errors\", \"No errors found for this client.\")\n            return\n        msg = \"\\n\".join([f\"{e['when']}: {e['type']} - {e['details']}\" for e in errors])\n        messagebox.showinfo(\"Recent Errors\", msg)\n\n    def quit(self):\n        self.kb.close()\n        self.master.quit()\n\n# -------------------- ENTRY POINT --------------------\n\ndef main():\n    DATA_DIR.mkdir(exist_ok=True)\n    root = tk.Tk()\n    app =     ''')\n        c.execute('''\n            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS test_scenarios (\n                id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n                client_id INTEGER,\n   c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute('''\n            SELECT e.error_type, e.error_details, e.occurred_at\n            FROM errors e\n            JOIN test_scenarios s ON e.scenario_id = s.id\n ANALYSIS & ERROR CATEGORIZATION --------------------\n\ndef analyze_output(input_df: pd.DataFrame, output_df: pd.DataFrame):\n    errors = []\n    # Check for missing columns\n    for col in input_df.columns:\n        if col not in output_df.columns:\n            errors.append({\n                \"type\": \"MissingColumn\",\n                \"details\": f\"Column '{col}' is missing in output.\"\n            })\n    # Check for row count mismatch\n    if len(input_df) != len(output_df):\n        errors.append({\n            \"type\": \"RowCountMismatch\",\n            \"details\": f\"Input rows: {len(input_df)}, Output rows: {len(output_df)}\"\n        })\n    # Check for value mismatches\n    common_cols = [col for col in input_df.columns if col in output_df.columns]\n    for   if in_val != out_val:\n                errors.append({\n                    \"type\": \"ValueMismatch\",\n                    \"details\": f\"Row {idx+1}, Column '{col}': input='{in_val}' output='{out_val}'\"\n                })\n    return errors\n\n# -------------------- IMPROVEMENT LOGIC --------------------\n\ndef build_gpt_prompt(client_name: str, previous_errors):\n    prompt = f\"Generate a new Excel test input file for automated test scenarios for client '{client_name}'.\"\n    if previous_errors:\n        prompt += \"\\nPrevious errors to avoid:\\n\"\n        for err in \"\"\"Handles SQLite-based RAG knowledge base for multi-client scenarios.\"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, db_file=DB_FILE):\n        self.conn = sqlite3.connect(db_file, check_same_thread=False)\n      id INTEGER PRIMARY KEY AUTOINCREMENT,\n                scenario_id INTEGER,\n                error_type TEXT,\n                error_details TEXT,\n                occurred_at TEXT,\n                FOREIGN KEY(scenario_id) REFERENCES test_scenarios(id)\n            )\n        ''')\n        self.conn.commit()\n\n    def get_or_create_client(self, name: str) -> int:\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute(\"SELECT id FROM clients WHERE name = ?\", (name,))\n        row = c.fetchone()\n        if row:\n            return row[0]\n        c.execute(\"INSERT INTO clients (name) VALUES (?)\", (name,))\n        self.conn.commit()\n        return c.lastrowid\n\n    def log_scenario(self, client_id: int, input_file: str, output_file: Optional[str], prompt: str,        VALUES (?, ?, ?, ?, ?, ?)\n        ''', (client_id, input_file, output_file, prompt, response, datetime.now().isoformat()))\n        self.conn.commit()\n        return c.lastrowid\n\n    def log_error(self, scenario_id: int, error_type: str, error_details: str):\n        c = self.conn.cursor()\n        c.execute('''\n            INSERT INTO errors (scenario_id, error_type, error_details, scenario data in CSV format.\"},\n                    {\"role\": \"user\", \"content\": prompt}\n                ],\n                max_tokens=1200,\n                temperature=0.2\n            )\n            csv_text = response['choices'][0]['message']['content']\n            # Use StringIO to read CSV from string\n            from io import StringIO\n            df = output file, compare with input, and categorize errors.\n    Returns a list of error dicts.\n    \"\"\"\n    errors = []\n    # Check for missing columns\n    for col in input_df.columns:\n        if col not in output_df.columns:\n            errors.append({\n                \"type\": \"MissingColumn\",\n                \"details\": f\"Column '{col}' is missing in output.\"\n            })\n    # Output rows: {len(output_df)}\"\n        })\n    # Check for value mismatches\n    common_cols = [col for col in input_df.columns if col in output_df.columns]\n    for col in common_cols:\n        for idx, (in_val, out_val) in enumerate(zip(input_df[col], output_df[col])):\n            if pd.isnull(in_val) and pd.isnull(out_val):\n                continue\n            if in_val != out_val:\n                errors.append({\n                    \"type\": \"ValueMismatch\",\n                    \"details\": f\"Row {idx+1}, Column '{col}': input='{in_val}' output='{out_val}'\"\n                })\n    return errors\n\n# -------------------- IMPROVEMENT LOGIC --------------------\n\ndef build_gpt_prompt(client_name: str, previous_errors: List[Dict[str, Any]]) -> str:\n    \"\"\"\n    Build a prompt for GPT-4, taking into account previous errors for improvement.\n    \"\"\"\n    prompt = f\"Generate a new Excel test input file for automated test scenarios for client '{client_name}'.\"\n output='3'\" in e['details'] for e in errors))\n\n    def test_null_handling(self):\n        df_in = pd.DataFrame({'A': [None, 2]})\n        df_out = pd.DataFrame({'A': [None, 2]})\n        errors = analyze_output(df_in, df_out)\n        self.assertEqual(errors, [])\n\n    def test_no_errors(self):\n        df_in = pd.DataFrame({'A': [1,2], 'B': [\"x\", \"y\"]})\n        df_out = pd.DataFrame({'A': [1,2], 'B': [\"x\", \"y\"]})\n        errors = analyze_output(df_in, df_out)\n        self.assertEqual(errors, [])\n\n\nclass TestBuildGPTPrompt(unittest.TestCase):\n    def
